<br />
Just from the sample, first impressions.<br />
<br />

Unlike sauvage edt or the elixir which can be cloying <br />
<br />
Least cloying out the line and actually one of the least cloying scents on the market. I‚Äôd say this is like 28+ but wear what you like. <br />
<br />
So far last ok but if you have an office job, sales or any job where you have to be around people and be presentable. This is a solid choice.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="95863"comment_id="2324064"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-Eau-Forte-95863.html?ccid=2324064#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2321580" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.8);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:3,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Is there a law that says flankers should smell exactly like the original?   Many times I have seen flankers dismissed by that reason only.    Additionally, this being a water based perfume, it gets an extra amount of hate.<br />
<br />
I blind bought it without seeing any reviews, and while waiting I did read many reviews and grew wary, thinking I bought a subpar product.   I almost canceled my order, but then decided to give it a try.<br />
<br />
Upon receiving it I immediately sprayed it my arm and was greeted by a most agreeable and elegant smell, woody, fresh and aquatic.   Also very strong smelling, so the water based bias was broken.  Yes, it is milky but it has to be like that, because it‚Äôs an emulsion of water and oil.   And no, it doesn‚Äôt stain your clothes.<br />
<br />
Drying out it gets more masculine and woody‚Ä¶.. and despite what many people say, it‚Äôs got the Sauvage DNA very much in there!<br />
<br />
If this bad hype and bad reviews continue, this fragrance might be heavily discounted in the future.   For me this a good thing, as I will continue using it I the foreseeable future.    I like it, and I recommend it.<br />
<br />
Don‚Äôt believe the bad hype.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="95863"comment_id="2305700"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-Eau-Forte-95863.html?ccid=2305700#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2304657" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:2,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1927010">The DZ</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-03">10/03/24 05:38</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>The response to this is fragcom at its absolute worst. Nobody was ever going to like this, even though it's extraordinarily likable. Those saying they had high hopes for a new Sauvage are quite dishonest. It's like a cinephile saying "I had such high hopes for The Matrix 3."<br />
<br />
It smells just like the note breakdown and still nods to the Sauvage line with the lavender and spices, though more abstractly. I expected the water-based part of this to be a kind of gimmick, but I actually ended up enjoying it. You spray it on and rub it in like a very fine lotion.<br />
<br />
Projection isn't strong, but I smelled it on myself all day--longevity on skin is ridiculous. I smelled it the next day. And I really enjoyed what I smelled. It's versatile, different, and I really could help but keep sniffing my arm. If you work in an environment where strongly projecting fragrances are frowned upon, this is a bonus. Sillage is moderate. Scent is extremely smooth.<br />
<br />
I'm really not trying to be contrarian. This is nice stuff, don't be scared by all the hate. It was always going to be received this way by the snobs. Give it time and fragcom people will start to speak positively about it. In the meantime, don't trust almost anything you read of anything you haven't smelled. Only the nose knows.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="95863"comment_id="2303340"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-Eau-Forte-95863.html?ccid=2303340#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2303171" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:1,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;female_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; The opening has a little freshness but all I can think of is sage.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="95863"comment_id="2295997"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-Eau-Forte-95863.html?ccid=2295997#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2295667" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2295667" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="HBeez"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1983639"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1983639.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="HBeez" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2295667ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2295667" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.88); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1983639">HBeez</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-26">09/26/24 07:38</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Tried this in store.<br />
<br />
I kinda like the opening, it's spicy, masculine, and has charachter and an edge. The dry down is less interesting, but still decent. I did notice something in it that smells like skin cream or ointment, so it's understandable that opinions are polarized. <br />
<br />
Performance is subpar. Projection is weak; it projects decently for an hour and then turns into a skins sent. However, longevity is above average, although in all honestly no one would be able to smell that skin sent so it's pointless longevity.<br />
<br />
I suspect the milky colour is due to an emulsifing agent that allows mixing of the fragrance oils with water, similar to how mixing dish soap with oil forms a milky solution. Likely due to the micelles forming a colloid solution that interact with light, similar to milk particles. More importantly, I suspect that the emulsifing agent "clings"/binds on to the fragrance molecules and prevents them from projecting, unlike alcohol which just evaporates and leaves the fragrance molecules to diffuse out of the oils. <br />
<br />
Now the real question, why did Dior release a water based fragrance? Do they really care about you and your possible skin reaction to a small amount of alcohol? I suspect not. If I were to bet, this is another attempt to cut cost. It might be cheaper to add a small amount of emulsifing agent than 80 ml of denatured alcohol. Yet they have the audasity to sell it for the same price as the parfum.<br />
<br />
Scent 7<br />
Performance 4<br />
Overall rating considering price 4</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="95863"comment_id="2295667"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-Eau-Forte-95863.html?ccid=2295667#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2294751" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2294751" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="caifan"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/939475"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.939475.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="caifan" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Cartier/Declaration-Parfum-48518.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.48518.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="D√©claration Parfum"title="D√©claration Parfum"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2294751ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2294751" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.75); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/939475">caifan</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-25">09/25/24 10:39</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Sauvage Eau Forte is an aromatic, spicy and woody fragrance.<br />
<br />
The opening is fresh and spicy, spices more similar to those used in the Elixir version than in other versions, as it smells a little like pink pepper and cardamom, accompanied by an aromatic lavender and some ambroxan, which is part of the DNA that preserves from the Sauvage line. As the minutes pass, musky and woody notes also emerge, but lavender takes the lead, giving a pleasant sensation of cleanliness.<br />
<br />
Sauvage Eau Forte can be used almost any season of the year, for informal situations or office work. It is not a unique aroma nor does it propose anything new, but for those who want a slight twist on the Sauvage DNA and smell different from any of the EDT, EDP or Parfum versions, it can be a good option.<br />
<br />
Its longevity is good, it stayed on me for almost 8 hours, however its aromatic sillage is less strong than others in the line, staying closer to the skin, but without having to get so close to the person wearing it.<br />
<br />
It has a pleasant and likeable smell, if I had used it without knowing it was a Sauvage or a Dior I would also say the same. However something that doesn't convince me is that it is water-based, since I understand that the "expiration time" of the fragrance is less than that of alcohol-based fragrances, so I suppose that whoever buys it will have to give it enough use, but for now that is just an assumption.<br />
<br />
My suggestion is you try this fragrance and have your own opinion.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="95863"comment_id="2294751"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-Eau-Forte-95863.html?ccid=2294751#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2294558" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2290156" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="ZeaMoore4"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1761519"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1761519.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="ZeaMoore4" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Rabanne/Invictus-Victory-65177.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.65177.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Invictus Victory"title="Invictus Victory"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2290156ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck3x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2290156" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.83); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1761519">ZeaMoore4</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-21">09/21/24 03:56</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Few fragrances get more hate than Dior Sauvage Eau Forte. I highly doubt half of the commenters have even tried it themselves. <br />
<br />
Yes, it is white and milky. No, you won't be covered in white milky gue for the rest of the day. It evaporates in 1-2 minutes, even on clothes. <br />
Because it's water based, it doesn't have the push off from alcohol. So the projection is a lot more consistent throughout the whole wear time. Longevity, i get about 6-8 hours. Nover a beast mode any point. But a nice scent bubble.<br />
<br />
It's a lot more green than i excepted from the notes. It's a pleasant smell for every day use. I'd say a fine casual scent, for work, or for when you can't have a monster fragrance on. I have to say it's a little overpriced. But it's Dior, so of course it's overpriced.  <br />
<br />
Personal score: 7/10. It's quite good, and i like it. But i'm in no hurry to get one, but if i see it on the used market or discount price, i may very well get it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="95863"comment_id="2290156"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-Eau-Forte-95863.html?ccid=2290156#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2289942" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.83);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2285457" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="chrisivE"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2191906"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="chrisivE" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Gucci/Gucci-Guilty-Absolute-43040.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.43040.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Gucci Guilty Absolute"title="Gucci Guilty Absolute"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2285457ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2285457" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.74); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2191906">chrisivE</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-17">09/17/24 00:20</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Sauvage Eau Forte by Dior opens with a refreshing and unique blend of minty, musky lavender, straying away from the citrusy profile typically associated with the Sauvage line. Instead, it feels more like stepping into a relaxing herb garden. The initial burst of lavender and mint pairs with balsamic and herbal undertones, possibly eucalyptus. As the fragrance evolves, musk becomes more dominant, with woody notes in the background‚Äîlikely sandalwood, cedar, or even palo santo‚Äîwhile elemi adds a resinous warmth that lingers throughout the wear.<br />
<br />
As the fragrance dries down, the elemi and musk take center stage, while the initial lavender and spices maintain a faint but noticeable presence. This combination creates a calming, aromatic profile, with woody nuances providing a comforting depth. The composition remains fairly balanced between its herbal and musky elements, making it stand out as a more tranquil interpretation of the traditional Sauvage DNA.<br />
<br />
<b>In short: A serene, herbaceous twist on the classic Sauvage. With mint, lavender, and musk leading to a woody, resinous base, it offers a refreshing and relaxing herbal garden scent that feels unique in its composition.</b></p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1350559">Ephemeris</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-16">09/16/24 21:56</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Honest review here since unfortunately people review bombed it in this website. <br />
<br />
Some say that this smells bad and i guarantee you thats not the case. <br />
It's actually such a beautiful composition and quite unique.<br />
<br />
I agree that it doesnt quite fit into the Sauvage lineup, but hey, you can always get the original if you like that style. And at this price point i strongly suggest that you do!<br />
<br />
The performance is average and the projection is weak at best. Still better than the "Parfum" version tough.<br />
Im happy that dior out of all brands is taking this kind of risk. But overall making non alcoholic fragrances is trying to solve a problem that doesn't exist. It's a gimmick.<br />
<br />
UPDATE!!: My theory is that I think after the Elixir got immediately cloned ( Asad came out like a week after which is crazy) Dior tried to make something thats more challenging for clone companies. They may come up with the similar smelling fragrance but i highly doubt that they can make this non alcoholic formulation. Not for a while at least. <br />
So for Dior this can be a genius move since almost all their fragrances are faked to perfection.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="95863"comment_id="2285379"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-Eau-Forte-95863.html?ccid=2285379#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2285231" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1195937">HungarianGenius</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-16">09/16/24 18:16</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I think its an impressively bold release from Dior. In an age when most younger guys seemingly want to smell either like a pre-teen girl or melted ice cream, releasing an unabashedly masculine fragrance is risky yet commendable. <br />
<br />
Eau Forte is simple but smells great, it opens as a punchy coniferous green musk and dries down to a refined and addictive spicy fougere, and for anyone familiar with the history of masculine perfumery, there's absolutely nothing off putting about it. The histrionic negative reviews below evaporate instantly the moment you smell it. <br />
<br />
Eau Forte hints at a number of other frags, FK own Narciso for Him, Sauvage obviosuly, and Invasion Barbare, in fact the drydown smells uncannily similar to Invasion Barbare without the vanilla.<br />
<br />
Finally the performance, its an absolute powerhouse, both intensity of scent and longevity. The alcohol free thing is a little goofy and neither here nor there for me, its not necessarily a negative, but i also dont see any positives.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; If you want a slight deviation from the original then look elsewhere.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="95863"comment_id="2280435"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-Eau-Forte-95863.html?ccid=2280435#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2279550" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.76);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />
It‚Äôs a nice masculine lavender + pine / woodsy + maybe some mint type fragrance. That powdery lavender reminds me of the very first time I bought and tried Kurkdjian‚Äôs JPG Le Male, probably back in 1999. Wow, unexpected. Kind of like you would not expect a Sauvage to smell like this.<br />
<br />
It does not have Sauvage DNA in my opinion. It does have Francis K DNA from the original Le Male times. To me, there is something ethereal, timeless, and possibly nostalgic about this scent.<br />
<br />
I really like it. Unless I get some negative reactions from significant others, I think it‚Äôs a keeper. Eau Forte appears to have minimal or zero ambroxan and is way more distinct and laid back.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="95863"comment_id="2278220"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-Eau-Forte-95863.html?ccid=2278220#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2277856" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.86);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; <br />

Putting on around 5-7 sprays at the department store, I would say it lasts for a good 4 hours before it's not detectable in the air, which I think is good for an alcohol-free fragrance. <br />

padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2276940" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="33christian33"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1454710"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="33christian33" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2276940ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2276940" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.75); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1454710">33christian33</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-09">09/09/24 09:14</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I'm convinced many who reviewed this have never even tried it.<br />
<br />
Look, if you're a fan of the classic sauvage with the aggressive sillage and sweet, punchy spices.. Then you won't enjoy this.<br />
<br />
This fragrance is definitely better for a more mature crowd who maybe wants something more subtle and soft.<br />
<br />
It's got that sauvage soapy DNA to it which is easily detectable. The opening has, what I can only describe as, a green element to it that makes it a little more fresh and woody.<br />
<br />
The drydown has a very nice creamy lavender and in some ways kind of reminds me of Armani code.<br />
<br />
This one is not going to project like crazy but you will have a really nice cozy bubble around you. It's one of those fragrances where you'll get a waft of it in the air but when you stick your nose to it on your skin it'll actually appear softer. Lasts a good 7 hours. This is perfect for the office and gym in my opinion.  <br />
<br />
I still personally like Sauvage Elixir more that this but for my style of fragrances this one is definitely up there. I cannot stand the EDT or Parfum.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="95863"comment_id="2276940"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-Eau-Forte-95863.html?ccid=2276940#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2276681" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2276681" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="ParfiuMen"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2248350"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="ParfiuMen" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2276681ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2276681" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.89); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2248350">ParfiuMen</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-09">09/09/24 04:19</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Tested it today. In order of observations:<br />
- Bottle - same old, nothing to comment on here.<br />
- Spray - often leaks. My hand would smell of it today and apparently, the issue is not only with the bottle I tried.<br />
- Top notes - Some people say they don't feel the lavender at all. For me, it is not only there, but there to stay. Intensive and overwhealming all over the other notes. Maybe a bit of a lime at the opening and, for sure, the feeling of a cream. Face or hand.<br />
- Medium notes - the "lime-y" feeling fades away after less than five minutes, leaving the lavender only. At least for me.<br />
- Base notes - still lavender. It's so powerful! The musk is overwhealmed by it, even 5 hours after the initial sprays. Seems long lasting with decent sillage. <br />
<br />
Now - I don't want to go with the crowd just for the sake of it. But this will be my least fav perfume from the Sauvage series. For sure will skip and my rate would be 5.5/10 tops. <br />
<br />
TL;DR: Lavender, overprices, can find something cheaper with the same notes.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="95863"comment_id="2276681"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-Eau-Forte-95863.html?ccid=2276681#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2276636" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:1,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="1"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2272837" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="ENP Hunter"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1373286"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1373286.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="ENP Hunter" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-Elixir-68415.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.68415.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Sauvage Elixir"title="Sauvage Elixir"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2272837ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck1x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2272837" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.7); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1373286">ENP Hunter</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-05">09/05/24 14:17</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Price breakdown: <br />
<br />
Sauvage Eau Forte (a parfum concentration): $193.00 for 3.4oz (100ml). <br />
Sauvage Parfum (a parfum concentration): $193.00 for 3.4oz (100ml). <br />
Sauvage Elixir (a parfum concentration): $193.00 for 2.0oz (60ml) or $255.00 for 3.4oz (100ml). <br />
<br />
It looks to me that the pricing is right in line with their other parfum concentrations. <br />
Lets look at a few others on the market: <br />
<br />
Bleu de Chanel Parfum (a parfum concentration): $193.00 for 3.4oz (100ml). <br />
Acqua Di Gio Parfum (assuming parfum concentration): $198.00 for 4.2oz (125ml). <br />
YSL Y Le Parfum (assuming parfum concentration): $190.00 for 3.4oz (100ml). <br />
Gucci Guilty Parfum Pour Homme (assuming parfum concentration): $183.00 for 3.0oz (90ml). <br />
Tom Ford Ombre Leather Parfum (you get the deal): $300.00 for 3.4oz (100ml), same for Costa Azzurra Parfum, Black Orchid Parfum, Grey Vetiver Parfum, etc. <br />
<br />
I am seeing a common theme here with designer brands marketing their fragrances at the $180-$200 price point, not including our friends over at Tom Ford, which no one seems to care about (predominantly because Tom Ford prices come down significantly on the gray market), which puts this fragrance not only standard for Dior, but for their competitors as well. <br />
The scent is slightly more masculine than FK typically produces, and the use of water as the perfume carrier using a unique emulsification method is a daring risk (one I find pretentious, but one none the less). <br />
The fragrance actually does perform as you would expect an actual parfum concentration to behave: it lasts all day on skin, but it doesn't project like a monster edt. Still, it does project within an arm's length for a good couple hours. After that, people are more likely to detect it in your scent trail rather than your mere existence (like it's older brother the Elixir, love that little nuke). <br />
I feel like you are going to see people, even on this incredibly obnoxious website, come back to this fragrance and go "huh, why did we hate this again? The price was the same as everything else, the scent performed pretty well, it was a creamy sweet lavender fragrance that wasn't like anything else on the market at the time (as evidenced by the smells like section), I wonder why I decided to hate this without smelling it?"<br />
<br />
Give it a try from an actual Dior tester bottle at a store. The atomizer changes the way the fragrance performs. If you dislike it, do so on the merits. If you like it, do so on the merits.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="95863"comment_id="2272837"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-Eau-Forte-95863.html?ccid=2272837#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2272603" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I finally tried this at a store, to say I'm surprised is an understatement. First off nothing about this is like anything in the Sauvage line. It is an overpowering musky spiciness which I think would do well in other scents but it just doesn't seem formulated well here.<br />
<br />

<br />
I can't speak on the longevity, I was too worried to spray this on my skin. The scent gets a 6.5/10 I couldn't see myself wear this.<br />

It's not as bad as I expected, on its own, it's pretty good, a green, aromatic musky scent, it's refreshing but the alcohol-free formula makes it last for only about 10 minutes, than it goes away. Try it for yourself, but don't get your expectations up, because it's absolutely not a Sauvage fragrance. What a shame, I would have expected Dior to make something more remarkable for their next release...</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="95863"comment_id="2271422"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-Eau-Forte-95863.html?ccid=2271422#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2271333" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; It does not have previous Sauvages DNA at all. It could be completely stand-alone scent.<br />
<br />
Performance: On paper it does not last too much. On skin it lasts for a long time. It has a lot of oils inside. Atomizer is finer than in EDT/EDP, etc, probably due to water. Projection is minimal.<br />
<br />
This 95% reminds me John Varvatos - Artisan Pure, but more refined. It has same soapy-aromatic-herbal scent.<br />
<br />
Overall it is a good scent, like Artisan Pure is not a bad scent, but it is not for everybody, although JV-AP priced 25-40 EUR for 125ml and Dior Sauvage eau Forte is 165 EUR for 100ml.<br />
<br />
Looking at recent MFK scents that I tested: 724 and Aqua Media Cologne forte, I can totally see the vibe of herbs in new Sauvage Eau Forte. I think he is fond of this direction as of now.<br />
<br />
Overall scent is okay, but I will not buy it, because it is boring. It is not a FK failure because he did a good job in terms of mixing ingredients. Dior or LVMH made this choice to put such product under Sauvage name and let down a lot of fans.<br />
<br />
I hope next FK scent will touch Dior Homme line or he will initiate a new line.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="95863"comment_id="2271333"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-Eau-Forte-95863.html?ccid=2271333#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2271279" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.77);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; (Store test)<br />
<br />

Eau Forte flanker refresh this in other direction that I really like.<br />
It is really Eau Forte (smell thin like Eau, but long lasting Forte).<br />
<br />
Sauvage Eau Forte dramatically reduce amount of Super-Amber, shift to soft musky woodsy side of thing.<br />
Still Pepper / Anis / Lavender and soft minerals amber still there resemblance Sauvage DNA.<br />
Still radiance out of my skin in very good manner and characteristic of each note cohesively play.<br />
<br />
Sauvage Eau Forte reminds me of current direction of Dior's fragrance. Dior Homme 2020.<br />
The woody dominant, musky fragrance combine with the original savage we know. Lavender / Pepper and Anis.<br />
I think this is hybrid Sauvage / Dior Homme in very good manner. It is balance and long-lasting.<br />
<br />
I notice spray heard slightly change and this one apply in very fine mist manner pretty much<br />
reminds me of Goutal's head spray. SA apply all over my arm with certain range and lightly tap in.<br />
The fragrance instantly dry on my skin without wet feeling.<br />
<br />
I really like release of Sauvage Eau Forte.<br />
I think this is great MFK refresh to original Sauvage DNA.<br />
<br />
A firm ok from me.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="95863"comment_id="2270061"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-Eau-Forte-95863.html?ccid=2270061#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2269974" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Longevity was good for me, lasted 11-12hrs and a shower before completely disappearing, projection was probably fine (?)</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="95863"comment_id="2268962"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-Eau-Forte-95863.html?ccid=2268962#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2268531" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.86);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:2,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Funnily the salesperson wasn't properly trained and said it was a body spray, lol. Anyway, I sprayed it on my arm and then waited to see how it would develop over time. It was not sticky or tacky on my skin. Just looked like milky water, but not sticky. I don't think it would stain clothes unless sprayed on them. <br />
It was really nice at first, fresh and almost minty after the Fahrenheit nods died down. After 3 hours it was virtually gone, with a slight soapy trace. I do think this would be nice in an intimate setting or while sweating it out on the dancefloor. <br />
It's nothing amazing and definitely overpriced. The water is for sure the gimic, and some people do want that option and everyone doesn't want a lot of sillage. It doesn't really remind me much of Sauvage and I hate Sauvage anyway (but love the Elixir).</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="95863"comment_id="2268531"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-Eau-Forte-95863.html?ccid=2268531#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2268425" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.71);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2089562">FragrancesAreFun</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-01">09/01/24 15:09</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Finally had the opportunity to sample it at Macy's.  Applied two sprays to the back of my hand - no fragrance applied this morning as I knew I would be able to obtain a sample and I did not want to have any other scents complicating matters.  My initial reaction is that white liquid globs were visible.  We left the store and I wanted to see how it developed.  After a half hour, I still had oil on my hand where applied.  Looked like mineral oil.  That certainly affects how and where it would be applied, if purchased.  Over time, I see that it is a very linear fragrance.  No real change over time.  Very potent, however.  And in a world where longevity is often lacking, this one does last.  Got home two hours later and asked my wife what she thought.  Ordinarily, she does not have strong feeling one way or another about my fragrances, but with this one, she took a good sniff, and pulled her head back. She really does not like it and I am not going to purchase a fragrance that my wife finds to be abhorrent.  I can see how it could be considered a flanker of Sauvage EDT and while it does not appear to have ambroxan, it does share that strong, nose overwhelming nature.<br />
<br />
I am still baffled why Dior made the business decision to make a water based fragrance. Is there market demand for this?  I can see a few extremely tiny markets:  (1) middle east where all alcohol is prohibited, (2) chemical dependency treatment centers where all alcohol is prohibited (hand sanitizer too as the addicts drink it), and (3) for those who are allergic to alcohol (and yet if allergic to alcohol likely they are allergic to fragrances too).  Every decision Dior/LVMH makes is a business decision, and this one is mystifying.<br />
<br />
Overall while I have great affinity for Dior and own and love many of their fragrances, this one is a solid pass.  I'm glad I had the opportunity to sample.  Purchasing this blind would have left me with a nearly useless bottle which I would have ended up giving away.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="95863"comment_id="2268425"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-Eau-Forte-95863.html?ccid=2268425#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2268327" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:2,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1733064">Adrianodiparigi</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-30">08/30/24 09:17</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>To start, I should mention that I have never worn Sauvage or any of its variations. I don't like blue fragrances, and I especially dislike ambroxan overdoses. Out of curiosity, I wanted to smell Kurkdjian's interpretation for his first mainstream Dior perfume. What was he going to do? Appeal to everyone? Surprise? Disappoint? Add his touch without turning it into an inaccessible niche fragrance? <br />
<br />
I don't have answers to all of these questions, but I can tell you what I felt. Eau Forte is a fresh, spicy, elegant, and reassuring fragrance all at once. It is clearly not a typical designer perfume. It‚Äôs closer to something Francis Kurkdjian could have released under his own brand. In that sense, it‚Äôs a bit less accessible. I think it‚Äôs aimed at a more mature audience. It‚Äôs a fragrance with strong projection for an hour or two, then it becomes a more subtle "aura" scent that you can smell on yourself all day long. Its water-based formula allows you to spray it liberally all over your body, as each spray emits a light, diffuse mist. This could very easily become a signature scent. I imagine a man in his 40s, well-off, elegant, confident, and likely at work. I feel like I would trust this guy. I think the fragrance will do very well in the Middle East as an easy grabber because it's alcohol-free. I could see myself wearing it at work or in transit between two VIP lounges. I can picture it less on a gym bro lifting weights.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="95863"comment_id="2265850"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-Eau-Forte-95863.html?ccid=2265850#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2265572" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.73);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;want&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1048023">leatherorrisviolet</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-29">08/29/24 19:31</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I could say so much about this one, but I will try to condense my review. TLDR this is a great, unique fragrance that is probably overpriced and incorrectly named <br />
<br />
People saying it smells nothing like Sauvage: good!! That is a positive thing!! If it smelled like Sauvage, everyone would say it‚Äôs a meaningless release that no one needed. This is something brand new, and I applaud MFK on that<br />
<br />
Speaking of MFK, I don‚Äôt think Sauvage Eau Forte would be getting anywhere near the criticism if it was a Demachy creation. It‚Äôs getting a bunch of criticism because it‚Äôs one of the first new MFK fragrances for Dior, and that kind of release naturally gets tons of hype before it even releases <br />
<br />
And speaking of the fragrance‚Äôs launch, the sample vials everyone got of this have skewed opinion and made everyone think this fragrance leaves white puddles on your skin. The only time I have gotten white puddles is when I use a cheap sample sprayer, when I am not spraying from the actual Dior bottle. Proof that you can‚Äôt fully judge a fragrance just by using a sample vial <br />
<br />
Regarding the smell itself: the smell makes me think of the niche brand Histoires de Parfums. It‚Äôs utterly addictive, but simultaneously never challenging or offensive. It‚Äôs rare that something so people pleasing is also able to keep my attention, but Sauvage Eau Forte pulls it off somehow <br />
<br />
Regarding projection: I have no idea. I am famously bad at judging this. What I can tell you is that I was able to smells this for 10 hours straight on my skin without having to lift my wrist to my nose. It provides an awesome scent bubble that is great for an office setting. As long as I am able to smell it without making an effort, that is all I care about. If I want compliments, there are so many loud choices for that. Sauvage Eau Forte is just for my own pleasure <br />
<br />
Regarding price: it costs too much, but it‚Äôs not like that is a unique thing nowadays for designer fragrances. I will wait for discounters <br />
<br />
And finally regarding the name: I understand why Dior would want to use an established name for this release, but I think this flanker would have fit better into the revamped Homme line or Fahrenheit line. Sauvage has some great releases but is ultimately a bro or frat line. Sauvage Eau Forte does not fit that description. If it were up to me, I would have called this Dior Homme Tonic or Fahrenheit Tonic and priced it lower since people are not used to water-based fragrances. Also an ad campaign with vintage and classically masculine vibes would do wonders for the sales. Have a guy wearing suspenders and hair pomade</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="95863"comment_id="2265319"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-Eau-Forte-95863.html?ccid=2265319#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2264848" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.7);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1822609">Kingofclubs</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-29">08/29/24 04:17</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Dear me Mr K, dear me.<br />
In his first major release as creative head of Dior Fragrances (yes he has worked on dior and in group for a while) there were a lot of expectations riding on this.<br />
Now Dior sell a bottle of Savage every 3 seconds, and whilst purists might sniffily dismiss it as a generic mall scent, it is undoubtedly still the best men's generic mall scent. Widest appeal and if a young man is asking what he should start with, we'll this is a good reference point (for us older dudes the choice gets more complex).<br />
Given how important the Savage line is within group (not just to Dior) updating the fragrance, selling bottles bearing the name, it has to be done right. I predict within 6 years this will be discontinued (bear in mind I'm no expert, and even experts are generally crap at predictions). Elixir was interesting but has really failed to shine and probably isn't cannibalism too many sales from its older brother. This certainly won't. Once the hype wears down, I expect this will remain a black mark against FK's record. BR540 shows this man is capable of a great mall scent (even though it isn't sold as such). People won't be in a rush to clone Savage Eau Forte. It's horrible.<br />
Even spraying it feels wierd, an unusual fine most leaving a milky secretion on the skin (please don't rub it in despite the temptation chided the girl on the counter). The opening is awful. Truly reprehensible. A really nasty minty/ eucalyptus note assaults the olfactive senses with a dry slap. It isn't even refreshing. It isn't immediately recognisable as being of Savage lineage. I can imagine there were reservations at board level. <br />
Given 40 minutes in the open air it eventually dried down to something almost, but not quite, resembling Elixir. Just not as strong or nice.<br />
Now Dior headline fragrances are the epitome of designer fragrances. Nearly anyone can pull them off with a solid base meaning it dries down predictably and in a way that is generally pleasing to most noses. No challenge, but so what? Collection Priv√©e is meant to satisfy the more discerning client.<br />
Credit does go for the technical achievement - from a manufacturing standpoint this is an innovative product, and Dior/LVMH group will be paying close attention. Maybe not to our reviews, but the sales figures in general. Perfume companies are ruthless, if this fails to ignite, it will in all likelihood be discontinued after a few productions runs, but it will be given time first. Bernard Arnault will be watching very carefully what is going on; a proruct that sells 3 bottles a second is way to precious.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="95863"comment_id="2264533"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-Eau-Forte-95863.html?ccid=2264533#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2264499" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.87);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="95863"comment_id="2264499"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-Eau-Forte-95863.html?ccid=2264499#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2263770" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2263770" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="JustMyVibe"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1606388"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1606388.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="JustMyVibe" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-Eau-Forte-95863.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.95863.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Sauvage Eau Forte"title="Sauvage Eau Forte"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2263770ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2263770" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.84); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1606388">JustMyVibe</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-28">08/28/24 10:56</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I just bought this recently and I've already recieved a few compliments. It's very different from rest of the sauvage line, the slight lavender and mass appeal being the only resemblence to the others. This could have easily been in a new line but it probably wouldn't be as successful. I understand what they are doing from a marketing standpoint and it makes sense. It seems like Francis Kurkdijian is taking a chance and trying to set a trend by making a non-alcoholic, water-based fragrance a part of one of the most iconic fragrance lines in modern perfumery, and I have to say I commend him for it. Flankers are well known to stray from the original scent. This is something companies have been doing for years and shouldn't be a surprise, nor should it be a strong consideration when deciding whether or not you like the fragrance. <br />
<br />
Now, onto the actual scent profile. It is a fresh, spicy, and woody fragrance with a bit of sweetness to smooth it out. It is definitely mass appealing, although I would not include this in the "blue" category of fragrances. It smells unique and original, but if I were to compare it to another fragrance I would say it reminds me a bit of Amyris Homme from MFK, except less sweet and more woody and spicy. <br />
<br />
Because this is a parfum extrait without inherently far projecting oils, it does not project far. Parfums typically don't project as far, but last longer than their EdT and EdP counterparts. This is why you might find that the Sauvage EdT projects more than any other entry into the line despite being less expensive. The low projecting nature of this fragrance makes this an excellent choice for a gentleman. This is no youthful fragrance bomb like the other entries in this line, although this scent can definitely be appreciated by young adults.<br />
<br />
Another surprising thing about this fragrance is the color of the product. The rest of the Sauvage line is clear but this one is milky white. The color is likely due to the use of water instead of alcohol and the use of natural oils, as oil-water emulsions tend to produce a milky white color. If you spray it properly you should not notice the color of it on your body, although the nozzle of the bottle tends to get splotches of white on it. <br />
<br />
All in all, this innovative fragrance strays even further from the line than the elixir does,  but this is not a bad thing. Forget names and labels, judge with your nose. Given that this is a Dior product at parfum concentration, I would say that the value is right on.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="95863"comment_id="2263770"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-Eau-Forte-95863.html?ccid=2263770#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2263743" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:3,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="3"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1158223">Prunel</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-28">08/28/24 10:25</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>It for sure isn't great imo, but it's not completely aweful. <br />
What's really disgusting is the fragrance itself, when you spray it it looks AWEFUL, little white drops that look like cream on a burnt skin. It also makes the sprayer get that milky sperm-like juice on it because it's simply falling on it.<br />
The scent is just ok. It smells like a woody musky fragrance with a bit of a "creamy" lavender, that's absolutely average. I don't think too many people would think this smells bad, this is pretty mass appealing. What's clear though is that performance is really not there. Maybe bottles need to macerate, but this doesn't project AT ALL. This is probably the flatest fragrance I've ever tried. It just stays on skin and that's it. <br />
I feel bad for Francis Kurkdjian, because he's a brilliant perfumer. I'm not sure if he's behind the idea, but sadly this doesn't deliver. The price is ABSURD and I find it really shocking that Dior let that reach the final stages of production. I guess it's good for people with skin issues, but you'll have to shower in it to smell it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="95863"comment_id="2263743"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-Eau-Forte-95863.html?ccid=2263743#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2263439" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; It's not the loud obnoxious ambroxan bomb that the edt or edp are, and really not related to those scents at all. It doesn't smell like the sauvage dna and doesn't smell like the elixir at all to me. I own the parfum and elixir and like them both. I may like this the best in the whole line though. Granted, I'm a middle aged guy.<br />
<br />
I think this could have been the beginning of a brand new line, and should have been. I just don't get the sauvage connection. This is even less related than the elixir to me.<br />
<br />
The quality of the materials smell better to me than any of the others in the line. Personally.<br />
<br />
Overall its a relatively unique but not groundbreaking scent. Clean, musky, spicy, almost soap-water fresh, with a base. Very little sweetness here. <br />
<br />
The longevity is great and the projection is moderate, but it has a heft to it. It's not thin or watery.<br />
<br />
Overall, a big like. 8/10.<br />
<br />
The water based thing is a little weird, not my thing per se, but it doesn't really hurt the wearing experience.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="95863"comment_id="2262776"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-Eau-Forte-95863.html?ccid=2262776#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2262616" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2262616" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="efendy"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1338068"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="efendy" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2262616ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2262616" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.88); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1338068">efendy</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-27">08/27/24 09:42</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I get why people are bashing the fragrance, the brand and/or the perfumer. I tried the fragrance myself two times this week and I really enjoy it. I like the scent itself and the performance isn't bad. I'm not entirely sure about it due to the water base. It smells very different on skin and on clothing. I specifically tested it on clothing to see if the milky and somewhat oily consistency would leave any visible stains. This is not the case. It seems to be absorbed completely by fabrics.<br />
<br />
Speaking about the price, I also find it way too high. If Dior wants people to try and buy this fragrance which they claim is revolutionary, then they really should have made it more accessible and affordable. On the other side, if a brand like Dior decides to do something tricky like a water based fragrance, I'm sure they know exactly what they're doing. Also I'm pretty sure they will make sure that it is better than any other water based fragrance produced before.<br />
<br />
We don't know if this was the perfumer's idea or something that the management ordered. Either way, he did a fantastic job in my opinion. I find it to be a very modern and unique smelling iteration of the original. It's not necessarily more masculine, but definitely resembles the original Sauvage in some ways. Contrary to others, I think it suits the Sauvage line very well.<br />
<br />
While the original gives me headache, Eau forte does not. I can keep smelling Eau forte all day long. However, I will have to test it more thoroughly to be sure about the performance. But at this point I am seriously considering buying a 60 ml bottle. I think this one will work both in warm and cold weather, so it seems to be a good well-blended allrounder. I guess most people hate if on the first sniff. I myself really like the opening, then the drydown gets a little harsh, almost iris-like. But after it has settled it turns into a nice smooth freshie, with a little milkiness to it.<br />
<br />
I wouldn't recommend blind buying, but I would however recommend to give it a serious try.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="95863"comment_id="2262616"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-Eau-Forte-95863.html?ccid=2262616#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2262384" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,245,242,0.86);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:1,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; The Elemi, spices and lavender mix really well to create something that is nowhere near Sauvage, but Dior Homme 2020 definitely right up the same DNA. <br />

I'm glad Mr. Kurkdjian gave this some depth than simply Ambroxab bomb. <br />
One last thing, longevity. It's not 30 minutes and it's gone. So far, it's been 7-8 hours on my usage. <br />
At the moment, it's not a "Love", but is a "Like". <br />
If this was in the Dior Homme line, it would've made much more sense, and would probably be liked by more people. It appears the fragrance community is flaming it, because it isn't similar to the rest of the Sauvage line, and isn't Alcohol based. People are automatically assuming it has Zero longevity. No, it isn't beast mode, but it isn't weak sauce either.
