padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2267298" class="cell small-2" ><div ><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="DiorHomme2015"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1752793"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1752793.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="DiorHomme2015" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2267298ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck5x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2267298" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"><div class="flex-child-shrink" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.75); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1752793">DiorHomme2015</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-31">08/31/24 13:48</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I don't usually post reviews, but I have to say that Eau Forte is better than people say. I tried it today and it smells nice. Don't listen to others, go try it. And longevity is pretty good.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="95863"comment_id="2267298"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-Eau-Forte-95863.html?ccid=2267298#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2241436" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2241436" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="ENP Hunter"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1373286"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1373286.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="ENP Hunter" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-Elixir-68415.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.68415.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Sauvage Elixir"title="Sauvage Elixir"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2241436ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck5x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2241436" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.74); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1373286">ENP Hunter</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-07">08/07/24 02:09</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Ladies and gentlemen, I am apparently about to go to war with the fragrance side of the internet. <br />
<br />
I am not a fan of Francis Kurkdjian‚Äôs work. I‚Äôm not a fan of metro/sweet/club fragrances such as most of the Le Male line, or his arguably even larger personal hit, BR540. I think that he specializes in synthetic sweet bombs that most younger men and women enjoy. And let me be clear, there is nothing wrong with that. However, it was my personal theory that he doesn‚Äôt particularly enjoy making ‚Äútruly‚Äù masculine fragrances, as it‚Äôs not his specialty and he doesn‚Äôt particularly identify with the concept of masculinity in fragrances, or at least doesn‚Äôt find it compelling. Again, there‚Äôs nothing wrong with any of that, and any artist is entitled to create that which they find compelling as much as it is up to the consumer to decide if they wish to engage with that kind of product. With that being said, I was concerned when he was announced as the new in house perfumer for Dior because I didn‚Äôt know how he would handle the Fahrenheit and Sauvage lines. Lines that, mind you, are unapologetically and even stereotypically masculine, each a masterpiece and testament to their respective generation‚Äôs interpretation of what ‚Äúmasculinity‚Äù smells like. I didn‚Äôt think he would do a good job, and I had very little faith. <br />
<br />
I was wrong. <br />
<br />
While shopping at Dillards I noticed that they just got in a tester for pre-sale. Apparently it officially comes in stock on the 15th. After seeing a couple videos on it, one of which being from Gents Scents, who did not like it much at all (I actually do respect his opinion heavily), I knew I had to test the fragrance for myself immediately. It‚Äôs worth noting that I am not interested in alcohol free formulas and think that they are a pointless gimmick, and I already had in my mind that even if this smells decent I‚Äôll hate it because of the texture and lack of performance. Expecting to hate it, being biased against FK, being biased against alcohol free fragrances, being biased against the scent itself by the content I consumed, I sprayed four long pressurized sprays onto the back of my hand, put it to my nose, and was shocked. <br />
<br />
It genuinely smells good. It smells cooling, it smells masculine, it smells clean, it smells like pepper, it smells like that Dior lavender: it smells like a Sauvage. I think the best way to describe it, and those who smell it down the line may very well agree, is that it is like (on my skin) a Dior Sauvage soda in the sense that it is sweeter like the edp, peppery, and effervescent. Then, in the dry down, it gets sweet and creamy on my skin and smells like a Sauvage Ice Cream. And here is the kicker gentlemen, it actually does perform acceptably well. It‚Äôs performance is no where near bad on my skin like other people are saying. I think the best way to describe the performance is that it‚Äôs not as fantastic as any of the other Sauvage scents, but, it‚Äôs stronger than the alcohol based fragrance known as Mont Blanc Explorer. It projects about arms length, and it lasts all day. Finally, the milky vibe isn‚Äôt as bad as you think it is. Dior atomizers aren‚Äôt like other brands. If you spray it the way it‚Äôs meant to be sprayed, it comes out in a delicate but large mist that throughly disperses the fragrances all over your skin. You don‚Äôt tap/click the sprayer like other fragrances. You strongly yet slowly spray, and you spray a good couple of times. I promise you, if you ‚Äúover spray‚Äù like you would a weaker fragrance such as Mont Blanc Explorer, you will be very happy with its performance. <br />
<br />
Overall, I‚Äôm going to give it an 8/10, eat my words about FK, and say that if you like the idea of a woody, lavender, Sauvage Ice Cream, this may be one you want to look into. Don‚Äôt believe the hate, and please test it yourself. <br />
<br />
Edit: Actually, the price point is standard market value for a parfum concentration. Dior Sauvage Parfum is $193 for 100ml, Sauvage Elixir is $193 for 60ml, and this is also $193 for 100ml. For the rest of the designer houses (Chanel, YSL, GA, Gucci, etc.), they range from around $180 - $200, with the exception of Tom Ford which charges $300 for 100ml parfum concentration versions of their mainline fragrances. I have therefore removed my negative comment regarding the price point.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="95863"comment_id="2241436"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-Eau-Forte-95863.html?ccid=2241436#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2278220" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;had&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2278220" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="FE2"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1871313"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1871313.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="FE2" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/TUMI/19-Degree-88381.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.88381.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="19 Degree"title="19 Degree"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2278220ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2278220" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.75); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1871313">FE2</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-10">09/10/24 12:22</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>After watching a couple of positive reviews among the sea of negative ones so far, I went and bought this and am wearing it.<br />
<br />
It‚Äôs a nice masculine lavender + pine / woodsy + maybe some mint type fragrance. That powdery lavender reminds me of the very first time I bought and tried Kurkdjian‚Äôs JPG Le Male, probably back in 1999. Wow, unexpected. Kind of like you would not expect a Sauvage to smell like this.<br />
<br />
It does not have Sauvage DNA in my opinion. It does have Francis K DNA from the original Le Male times. To me, there is something ethereal, timeless, and possibly nostalgic about this scent.<br />
<br />
I really like it. Unless I get some negative reactions from significant others, I think it‚Äôs a keeper. Also, I don‚Äôt own any other Sauvage because the DNA is overly popular, has too much ambroxan, and I have other alternatives to the Elixir. Eau Forte appears to have minimal or zero ambroxan and is way more distinct and laid back.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="95863"comment_id="2278220"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-Eau-Forte-95863.html?ccid=2278220#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2263770" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2263770" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="JustMyVibe"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1606388"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1606388.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="JustMyVibe" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-Eau-Forte-95863.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.95863.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Sauvage Eau Forte"title="Sauvage Eau Forte"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2263770ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2263770" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.75); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1606388">JustMyVibe</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-28">08/28/24 10:56</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I just bought this recently and I've already recieved a few compliments. It's very different from rest of the sauvage line, the slight lavender and mass appeal being the only resemblence to the others. This could have easily been in a new line but it probably wouldn't be as successful. I understand what they are doing from a marketing standpoint and it makes sense. It seems like Francis Kurkdijian is taking a chance and trying to set a trend by making a non-alcoholic, water-based fragrance a part of one of the most iconic fragrance lines in modern perfumery, and I have to say I commend him for it. Flankers are well known to stray from the original scent. This is something companies have been doing for years and shouldn't be a surprise, nor should it be a strong consideration when deciding whether or not you like the fragrance. <br />
<br />
Now, onto the actual scent profile. It is a fresh, spicy, and woody fragrance with a bit of sweetness to smooth it out. It is definitely mass appealing, although I would not include this in the "blue" category of fragrances. It smells unique and original, but if I were to compare it to another fragrance I would say it reminds me a bit of Amyris Homme from MFK, except less sweet and more woody and spicy. <br />
<br />
Because this is a parfum extrait without inherently far projecting oils, it does not project far. Parfums typically don't project as far, but last longer than their EdT and EdP counterparts. This is why you might find that the Sauvage EdT projects more than any other entry into the line despite being less expensive. The low projecting nature of this fragrance makes this an excellent choice for a gentleman. This is no youthful fragrance bomb like the other entries in this line, although this scent can definitely be appreciated by young adults.<br />
<br />
Another surprising thing about this fragrance is the color of the product. The rest of the Sauvage line is clear but this one is milky white. The color is likely due to the use of water instead of alcohol and the use of natural oils, as oil-water emulsions tend to produce a milky white color. If you spray it properly you should not notice the color of it on your body, although the nozzle of the bottle tends to get splotches of white on it. <br />
<br />
All in all, this innovative fragrance strays even further from the line than the elixir does,  but this is not a bad thing. Forget names and labels, judge with your nose. Given that this is a Dior product at parfum concentration, I would say that the value is right on.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="95863"comment_id="2263770"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-Eau-Forte-95863.html?ccid=2263770#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div>                            <reviews-infinity :random-colors="[&quot;#fefcee&quot;,&quot;#faf7ec&quot;,&quot;#f9f9f3&quot;,&quot;#f8f9ec&quot;,&quot;#fffdea&quot;,&quot;#faf9fb&quot;,&quot;#faf5f2&quot;,&quot;#f7f4f2&quot;]" :perfume-id="95863" sentiment="positive"></reviews-infinity>

padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2232781" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="EbagAppez"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1919507"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.1919507.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="EbagAppez" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Gucci/Gucci-Guilty-Intense-Pour-Homme-13075.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.13075.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Gucci Guilty Intense Pour Homme"title="Gucci Guilty Intense Pour Homme"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2232781ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck7x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2232781" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(254,252,238,0.88); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1919507">EbagAppez</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-29">07/29/24 10:41</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I rarely dunk on things hard when it comes to reviews, just look at any of my other reviews and you will see I'm not a troll or hater. If I strongly dislike a fragrance, I will always write out the actual justification for the poor rating.<br />
<br />
Heck, I am also a fan of the Sauvage product line. But, unfortunately, as a frustrated consumer, something has to change in the fragrance industry sooner than later! <br />
<br />
Maybe if more people began speaking out, these brands might just wake up a little bit from their cash-grab business models.<br />
<br />
I was initially excited to see what Kurkdijan was going to do with this release. But the minute I saw that they were going with a water based frag, I already had my reservations. If you ever experienced Azzaro Chromes Under the Pole water based product, then this will deliver the same underwhelming experience.<br />
<br />
I sampled this at the store today both on skin (mistake) and on paper. <br />
<br />
The white sticky globs of fragrance this leaves behind are really unbecoming and leave my arm feeling tacky and some of my hairs sticking together.<br />
<br />
What is even worse than the odd appearance and feel of the product on both of my forearms is the disasterous performance! <br />
<br />
I am a fan of Sauvage, but, for the price they are asking this is completely unacceptable. They have it listed as a parfum concentration, but this stuff performs like an Eau de Cologne or Eau Fraiche! At best on paper/clothes, you might get 4-5 hours with this product. On skin you're probably looking at 3-4 hours. The projection immediately starts out as a 6 inch bubble, maybe a foot if you're lucky. After an hour it's already a skin scent.<br />
<br />
If this was a $20-$30 fragrance, then the pedestrian scent profile, and lackluster performance would be just passable. BUT for $200+ this is unacceptable as a consumer.<br />
<br />
Personally, for my taste, this is a major pass. I wouldn't even want a free bottle for my own personal use.<br />
<br />
If you plan on getting yourself a bottle of Sauvage, get the Parfum or EDP and stay away from this thing.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="95863"comment_id="2232781"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Dior/Sauvage-Eau-Forte-95863.html?ccid=2232781#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2232807" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:1,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:1,&quot;sillage&quot;:1,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="1"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%;
